Transportation permits will be suspended. After the meeting, it was adjourned immediately.

Nantong 73

Indignation of All Circles Against Japan: All circles in Nantong are furious about the Japanese dispatch of troops to forcefully occupy Manchuria. At 1:00 PM on the 22nd, more than 5,000 people gathered at the public sports field in the south of the city to hold a mass rally. It was decided to send a telegram of support and strictly enforce economic severance with Japan. The crowd was indignant. After the meeting, they marched through the streets to urge everyone to pay attention.

Sea Bandits Land and Burn and Kidnap: More than 300 sea bandits from Lüsi landed in Sanjia Town and robbed wildly. When fishermen refused to pay fees, they set fire to boats. The police and local militia went to intercept them. The bandits kidnapped Peng Shaoan and six women from the town and escaped by boat. The coastal area has recently been extremely panicked.

Judgment on the Discount of Cash Coins for Silver Dollars: The Nantong County Education Bureau deposited public funds in a money shop. When converting cash coins into silver dollars, they insisted on calculating the price of silver dollars according to the exchange rate at the time of deposit. The money shop refused and sued the court, requesting that the conversion be calculated according to the market price. The court ruled on the 22nd that the plaintiff's (money shop's) lawsuit was rejected.

Gaoyou 74

The County Government Orders All Bureaus and Fields to Expedite Handover: The County Government previously received an order from the Provincial Government to take over all bureaus and fields. The four bureaus of education, finance, public security, and construction will be reorganized into departments. It is learned that all bureaus and fields received express mail telegrams from various departments today (the 21st), ordering them to expedite the handover and submit them to the County Government for acceptance.

District Chief Accused and Summoned for Trial on a Scheduled Date: Wan Diankui, the District Chief of the First District of this county, was accused of blocking the river mouth dams, cutting corners, and neglecting the lives and property of the entire city. Huang Shaochen, Shen Liqing, and Zhang Shihua, three citizens of this city, jointly filed a complaint with the County Government. It is learned that the County Government has scheduled a court hearing on the 26th of this month.

Yangzhou 75

Eleven Trade Associations Telegraph the Department to Oppose House Rent Surtax: The eleven trade associations of Jiangdu, including oil, sauce, firewood, inn, medicine, wide goods, silk, rice, tea food, and tea leaves, and southern goods, because of the County Political Conference, Finance Bureau Chief Dong Digu, proposed the method of levying house rent surtax for relief funds, collecting two months' rent to make up for the local budget deficit. It was decided to submit the detailed method to the Finance Bureau, convene all French for discussion, and then submit it to the Department for approval. The County Bureau also convened a meeting of various groups, agencies, and banks on the 14th to discuss the matter. The result of the discussion was that the house rent surtax should also be levied. Therefore, on the 21st, a joint meeting was held, deciding to telegraph Hu, the head of the Civil Affairs Department, on the 22nd, stating the merchants' difficulties and proposing that the principle of house rent surtax was based on the corrupt practices of warlords and should not be imitated under the Party's rule. Therefore, after a joint meeting of the trade associations, it was decided that before the house rent surtax is implemented, the Department should be telegraphed first, requesting Jiangdu County to forward the message to the Finance Bureau and dispel the original proposal for the house rent surtax.

Shangyu 76

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Yuan Village: Xu Wenxue's family in Ruan Village, Fifteen Township, South Township, was broken into by more than 20 bandits armed with wooden-cased guns on the night of the 14th. Xu's 14-year-old grandson, Guo Sheng, was kidnapped, and 200 silver dollars and countless clothes were robbed. A letter was left demanding 50,000 yuan. They were given five days to send someone to Dalanshan to redeem him, otherwise, they would tear up the ticket and burn the house. Xu's family was panicked and had no way to deal with it.

Negligence of Duty Causes Death: Zhu Yunqiao, a resident doctor at the Zhang Zhen Dexintang Pharmacy, had previously prescribed the herb Asarum for Feng Jiucheng's 14-year-old son, Minyao, from Nanbu Village. He prescribed as much as two qian. After Minyao took it, his condition worsened drastically overnight, and he died. Jiucheng was heartbroken and asked the medical community to comment on the prescription. Everyone said that Asarum is a strong medicine, and adults can only use one qian at most. Now, a child over ten years old was given as much as two qian, so it was difficult to save his life. Feng became even more grief-stricken when he heard this. Recently, he hired a lawyer to draft a lawsuit against the county.

Special Report on Educational News

Suggestions for Concrete Implementation Methods for Elementary Schools to Resist Japan and Save the Nation 77

By Hu Shuyi

As the Japanese take advantage of our natural disasters and engage in violent acts, deploying troops to seize territory, news of these atrocities spreads, causing righteous indignation among all those with blood and breath. It is fitting that each person should express their views and fulfill their responsibilities, jointly devising methods to resist Japan and save the nation. Based on my observations and understanding within the education sector, I have drafted this article to express my personal desire to save the nation. I hope that comrades in elementary education across the country will continue to study, add to, and correct it. This method is conceived based on the actual environment of domestic elementary schools, focusing on practical application rather than theoretical discussion. It is now presented in the following sections:

(1) Teaching: Instruction should begin with the recent incident of the Japanese army's dispatch of troops to invade and occupy Fanyang, using "Researching Japan" as the central theme of teaching. Every effort should be made to integrate various subjects. For example, in the Chinese language class, select readings or review records or reports of the Japanese army's violence. In composition, children can be asked to write propaganda to encourage compatriots to rise up and resist Japan to save the nation. In social studies, the Japanese invasion plan and the history and geography of the Eastern Provinces and the South Manchurian Railway can be studied. In arithmetic, the area of the Eastern Provinces, the number of Japanese troops, and statistics on various losses in the Eastern Provinces can be calculated. In art, children can be asked to draw imaginative pictures of the Japanese army's violence, and to create various anti-Japanese propaganda. In natural science, the resources of the Eastern Provinces and South Manchuria, and the manufacture of bullets and gunpowder can be studied. In calligraphy, practice writing leaflets and slogans. In physical education, practice various anti-Japanese fitness exercises. In singing, sing various songs about joining the army or resisting Japan. The goal is to focus each subject on resisting Japan and saving the nation, imperceptibly achieving anti-Japanese training in teaching. The above is just a brief example, and of course, can be varied and adapted as needed.

(2) Training: Several ideas have come to mind; here is one example: 1. Report on the Japanese army's violence and active national salvation methods during memorial weeks.

2. Hold morning meetings every day to report to all children on the investigation of various Japanese goods.

3. Class teachers should talk regularly, promoting active national salvation methods to children.

4. Edit children's wall newspapers, making full use of pictures to arouse their enthusiasm for resisting Japan and saving the nation.

5. Train children to actively save money to save the nation. Set up a "saving money" fund in each class, using competitions to encourage them to save pocket money and cultivate the habit of saving. This saving money still belongs to each individual child, and should be deposited in a reliable local bank for special protection, to be used when urgently needed to save the nation.

6. Actively train children to endure hardship, using competition to motivate them.

7. Actively promote healthy exercise for children, using competition to promote it.

8. Stipulate a minimum level of fitness. Students who do not meet the corresponding passing standard will not be promoted or graduate.

9. Hold essay or speech contests, with specific plans to resist Japan and save the nation as the central topic.

(3) Teaching Materials: Here is an example of what has come to mind. Detailed teaching materials for resisting Japan and saving the nation should be edited and distributed.

(1) Nursery rhymes: List the facts of the Japanese army's violence in the Eastern Provinces and compile them into nursery rhymes.

(2) Supplementary teaching materials: Compile the Japanese plans to invade Manchuria and Mongolia and the circumstances of the recent Japanese army riots into supplementary teaching materials, with one incident as one topic, compiled into a small booklet. The language should be simple and clear so that children can read freely.

(3) Scripts: Compile the recent sudden occupation of Liaoji by Japanese soldiers into scripts for elementary school students to perform.

(4) Stories: In the lower grades, stories can be compiled for teachers to use as reference lectures. In the higher grades, they can be used as extracurricular reading material.

(4) Administration: The principal should formulate a teaching calendar for resisting Japan and saving the nation, proceeding daily without any steps being missed. Here is an example of what has come to mind:

(1) Stipulate the central training issue for each day and notify teachers to implement it.

(2) Stipulate the order of faculty meetings and the central points of discussion.

(3) Stipulate the steps and methods for visiting guest families and implement them regularly.

(4) Stipulate the steps for teaching and training and implement them in stages.

(5) Stipulate the number of children's gatherings and the key points of their talks.

(6) Stipulate methods for checking children's health and the steps for carrying them out.

(7) Compile tests to measure the results after implementation.

(8) Conduct regular liaison with other schools and implement active and concrete methods.

(9) Review various anti-Japanese and national salvation teaching materials.

(10) Stipulate other emergency steps and plan for them regularly.

The various methods listed above, whether for urban or rural schools, should not encounter any difficulties in practice. However, how to adapt them to the actual environment of each school will naturally require careful consideration and change. The author is only promoting a method or using it to stimulate further research by experts to obtain more concrete and active methods to resist Japan and save the nation, which is the only hope.

Universities Will Go on Strike and Petition

The Shanghai University Students Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee held its first Executive Committee meeting yesterday afternoon at the Soochow University Law School on Kunshan Road. The meeting began at 3:00 PM, chaired by Liu Xuantian and recorded by Zhong Liangfang. The following resolutions were passed on the spot: (1) All universities in the city will go on strike from this Saturday (the 26th). On Sunday (the 27th), each school will send two representatives to the National Government in Nanjing to petition, requesting the concentration of national military power to resist the Japanese troops in the Eastern Provinces. The resumption of classes will be decided after the representatives returning to Shanghai from Nanjing convene a representative assembly to make further decisions. (2) The executive committee members from the eleven schools of Chih Tze College, Political Science College, Great China University, Fudan University, Kwang Hua University, Jiaotong University, Datong University, Shanghai Law School, Soochow University, Tungwen College, and Labor University will be designated as secretaries of this committee to organize a secretariat, accept the resolutions of the representative assembly, and proceed with implementation. (3) The representative assembly is the highest authority of this committee. After the secretariat is established, various specialized committees may be established to handle committee affairs depending on the scope of future affairs. (4) Fudan University will draft a declaration, and Great China University, Soochow University, and Hujiang University will draft organizational laws for temporary adoption. After review and revision by the executive committee members of Jiaotong University and Fudan University, they will be submitted to the secretariat for voting. It was reported that the strike issue was discussed for a long time during yesterday's meeting, and the opinions of the various schools were inconsistent, so the motion was not decided until two hours later.

The Thoughts of Overseas Chinese Students in Japan on the National Games 95

| Busy Raising Funds to Relieve Flood Disasters | Difficult to Raise Funds Again Due to Economic Downturn |

Baseball's Inability to Return Home is a Pity

(Special Correspondent) Last spring, the Kobe Chinese YMCA basketball team participated in the grand event of the first National Games, which was well received by the government and sports circles. After returning to Japan, they trained even harder and their skills improved rapidly. Last winter, in the Hanshin area, they repeatedly defeated Kansai Gakuin, Kobe Westerners, and Konan High School and other strong teams, winning the championship for three consecutive years, bringing glory to our overseas Chinese. In the early summer of this year, when Santo Tomas from the Philippines came to Japan, the Japan Basketball Association selected the Chinese YMCA team to compete with them, which proves that its strength is also deeply recognized by the Japanese. This time, the second National Games have been postponed frequently. The overseas Chinese feel distressed about the tragic damage caused by the floods in their motherland, and they believe that it is imperative to help compatriots in need. Although it is a time of economic downturn, they are all actively raising funds. A few days ago, the Consul General in Hanshin received a telegram from the National Games Organizing Committee, asking whether there were any overseas Chinese representatives participating. After careful discussion by those with lofty ideals in the sports world, it was concluded that it is appropriate to express condolences and sympathy for the disasters in the motherland. The original plan to send baseball and basketball teams back to the country to attend was shelved. The attitude of the decision is commendable. I wonder what the people in the country feel.

However, the most regrettable thing is that the overseas Chinese baseball team cannot return to the country and bury their good skills overseas. Overseas Chinese students in Japan have always been fond of this skill, and the team has a prestigious history. In recent years, stimulated by the progress of the Japanese, they have studied more seriously and trained harder. To be fair, their baseball skills are better than the Xiangshan Chinese team. To date, outstanding talents who have returned to the country and shown their skills in Hong Kong and Shanghai include Li Chenglan, Guo Rixian, and Zeng Guangbang. Others, such as the veterans Zhao Shilun, Huang Jiaojian, and Zhang Wu, although they have retired, were also fierce generals on the field in the past. Currently, Liu Sezhang (Hosei University) and Bao Guanda (Nanjing Institute of Technology) in Yokohama, the Cui brothers Ri Guang and Ri Fu (Yokohama Commercial), and Liang Wuxiong (St. Joseph's College) are all young student athletes. Others, such as Liang Chengsong, Bao Hui, and Zheng Sipei (pitcher), Zeng Guangchao (shortstop), Zheng Bohan (outfielder), and He Jinben (third baseman) of the Kobe Chinese team, although they have joined the business world, are still young and strong, and their skills are extraordinary. If we combine the elites of the two ports to organize an overseas Chinese baseball team in Japan to participate in the second National Games in Nanjing, the championship will definitely be won. Therefore, since the Japanese overseas Chinese cannot attend, the domestic teams in Hong Kong, Shanghai, and Tianjin must not be complacent and complacent. I hope that everyone will work hard to promote the development of this skill and prepare for the challenge of the Japanese overseas Chinese next year or the year after. The future is bright, and I hope that all people in the baseball world will work together.

Heartbreaking Words 97

— Du Juan

Dear compatriots, this is not the time for singing and dancing. The violent Japanese soldiers have already invaded our land, plundered our property, and massacred our compatriots. Do you have a heart and blood? Then you should emulate Goujian and work together to sleep on brushwood and taste gall.

Those Who Do Not Eliminate the Weeds in the Courtyard Merely Engage in Empty Talk

Tolstoy and the Followers of Muhammad 98

Yue Wumu said: "If civil officials do not love money and military officials do not fear death, the world will be at peace." This time, the Japanese violated international law and invaded the Northeast with heavy troops, which is no less than an act of robbery. Military officials should be as willing to die as they are to defend the country and protect the people. Who knew that some military officials would adopt a policy of non-resistance and become followers of Tolstoy. Ask him: "If the Japanese soldiers occupy Shenyang, will you not resist?" He said, "Do not resist!" Ask him: "If the Japanese soldiers occupy Jilin, will you not resist?" He said, "Do not resist!" Ask him: "If the Japanese soldiers want you, your parents, wives, children, and friends to be slaves, will you not resist?" He said, "Do not resist!" Ask him: "If the Japanese soldiers bury all the Chinese alive in mass graves, will you not resist?" He said, "Do not resist!" What a thorough follower of Tolstoy! But he is following Muhammad's tactics with his own family, holding the Koran in his left hand and a sword in his right to suppress his compatriots. On that sword, the blood of his fifteen- or sixteen-year-old younger brother has not yet dried!

American Silver Also Sees Contraction P] 99

Yesterday (the 22nd), a dispatch from New York stated that the price of American silver had retreated to 62.5, which equates to a spot price of 2 shillings and 8 pence and 625/1000. The exchange rate of British pounds to US dollars fell by 2 cents, to $4.23. The exchange rate of US dollars to British pounds dropped by 1 shilling and 2 pence, to £4.20. The exchange rate of Japanese yen to US dollars rose by 1 shilling and 7 pence, to ¥49.30. The exchange rate of British pounds to Japanese yen soared by 4 shillings and 32/29 pence, to 2 shillings and 5 pence. The spot price in Mumbai rose by 1 rupee and 0.03 anna, to 48 rupees and 0.08 anna. The forward price also rose by 2 annas, to 47 rupees and 0.08 anna. The market is said to be fluctuating and unstable, and the money market is becoming increasingly tight.

Tightening Money Market

Due to the influence of the current political situation, the money market has experienced an emergency in recent days. Because of the general trend, we have not dared to fully discuss the inner workings of this tightening situation, fearing that it would attract attention and cause misunderstandings, leading to special disturbances. At a time of national crisis, financial panic is inevitable. It is fortunate that those in charge are doing their best to maintain stability.

Exchange Rates (Silver Tael)

The morning market was at 7 yuan 2 fen 5 li 1 hao 2 hu and a half. The afternoon market increased by half a li, to 7 yuan 2 fen 5 li 6 hao 2 hu and a half. The result was a decrease of 3 hao and 7 hu and a half compared to the previous day. (Silver Exchange) The morning market was 3 qian and 5 fen, and the afternoon market was 4 qian, an increase of 1 qian and 4 fen compared to the previous day. Bank rates suddenly rose to 6 qian and 4 fen, and the "hua tou" (commissions) increased from 3 qian and 5 fen to 4 qian, eventually closing at 3 qian.

Securities Diplomacy Enters Desperate Situation Securities Fall Sharply Again 100

Although the Financial Industry Does Its Best to Absorb and Maintain the Market, How Can the Declining Trend Be Reversed? The Rate of Decline Is Becoming More Severe 101

Yesterday (the 23rd), the situation of various prices in the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange market was that, due to the continuous invasion of the Japanese army and the expansion of our country's territory, the extent of their looting and massacres was even greater than before. All constructions in the provinces of Liaoning and Jilin were destroyed. Diplomatic contact has become impossible. War clouds are dense, and a breakdown may be unavoidable, and this may involve international relations, which makes the danger even greater. The securities market is in such an environment that it is difficult to recover in a short time. When the market opened yesterday morning, people were in a vacuum, and the market was selling off universally. The selling and resale transactions were like a tidal wave, and the tension and seriousness of the market were no less than last weekend. All bonds were under pressure, and all fell sharply. If there had not been a large amount of short covering and the financial industry in Shanghai had not done its best to absorb and maintain the market, then the bonds would have fallen and trading would have been suspended in the morning. However, because the salt tax in September fell too much, trading was suspended, and the after-market was extended to 5 pm due to the need to chase the evidence. At that time, the people in the market were as panicked as before, and there was no slight change in the bond market environment. The market prices of various bonds became even lower than the previous market trend, which led to almost all bonds falling and trading being suspended. Only a few types, such as the 96 series of disarmament bonds due next month and the 10 series of troop reduction bonds with September tariff, did not fall to the point of suspension. However, after the suspension of trading, although there were dark market transactions among brokers, there was not much to be heard, and the price was static, only about half a yuan around the suspension price. It is still not optimistic to view the bond market situation. The trend will depend on whether there is a turnaround in the diplomatic situation. It is estimated that the total transaction volume of futures for the whole day reached about 32 million yuan, and there was no market for spot goods.

Brisk Buying in the Yarn and Cotton Yarn Market

The yarn market is unusually chaotic, with a mixed and confusing situation, and prices are rising and falling unevenly, but the buying trend is very strong. Due to the economic severance with Japan, the trading of local yarn has greatly improved, so people are shaken, and Japanese merchants are massively buying to cover short positions, and the market is becoming increasingly tight. However, a certain major merchant has slightly sold to flatten the market price, but this trend is difficult to calm down in a short time.

"Ren Biao" (Human Standard) Traders Rush to Cover Short Positions

At the opening of the "Ren Biao" market, due to the Japanese army's invasion of Northeast China, people's spirits were high, and Japanese merchants were buying to cover short positions, with prices rising by 3, 4, and 5 taels in each month. In the second session, a large trader sold, and the market price fell sharply by 3 taels. The result was an increase of 1 tael and 7 or 8 qian. In the afternoon, the situation was slightly calmer, with the near months rising by 2 or 4 qian. The trading volume totaled 80,000 bales. The trading volume in the afternoon was not recorded. It was found that the sales were: Mei Ji 300 bales, Rong Xing over 2,700 bales, Ming Hua 1,150 bales, Heng De 1,250 bales, Shen Ji 2,600 bales, Yi Chang 1,150 bales, Yi Yu 1,950 bales, Xin Cheng 4,150 bales, and De Ji 1,050 bales. The purchases were: Rui Da 10,750 bales, Da Fu 1,450 bales, Da Feng 1,150 bales, Gong Da 3,800 bales, Tian Jiang 2,500 bales, Shen Chang 1,850 bales, Chang Feng 3,900 bales, and Yong Chang 1,250 bales. Cotton Market Rises Sharply in the Evening Session

The cotton market was flat in the morning, but trended upward in the afternoon. The market atmosphere was very chaotic, but American cotton continued to be depressed, and gold prices were also softening. Moreover, the selling price of foreign cotton was very cheap, so large speculators continued to sell. However, the yarn market was firm, and the cotton market was driven by it. Most retail investors, fearing that the Japanese army's violent invasion of Northeast China would expand the trend and foreign cotton could not be imported, purchased more to go long. However, foreign cotton prices are very cheap, and the outlook is still mostly bearish.

Grain: River Rice Drop, Wind Temporarily Settled

The sources from Nantou yesterday were not many, and the remaining stock in the docks was also scarce. The sales in urban and rural stores turned slack, and fresh goods were slightly moving. The market for thick japonica rice was settled. Although there were not many thin indica rice goods, the buyers were still sluggish. Only the freshest rice was picked in this street, and the middle-grade rice was still sluggish, causing the price to fall. However, considering the long distance between inside and outside, there may be a hope of stabilization. The market for old Luoyang glutinous rice was weak, and the goods were also sporadic, temporarily presenting a flat image. The market for new Luoyang glutinous rice was firm due to the sharp price drop. The market for new japonica rice was rare and sales were weak.

New Gate: Yesterday, due to the unfavorable weather, goods arrived on the 20th or 30th of the month, and the trend was declining. Thick japonica rice and early and late indica rice opened at a higher price of 2 jiao in the morning. Due to the continuous sharp drop in the price of new Luoyang glutinous rice, the arrival of goods must be scarce, and the market was stable. The market for old Dujiang glutinous rice was slightly active, but the buyers were also sluggish, and the situation was downstream. There was a very strong demand for general transformation of Yuan tea food stores, and the situation was firm.

Foreign Rice Market Turns Better in the Afternoon

Yesterday, the spot market for foreign rice was flat, and the futures market turned better because foreign firms received large telegrams and the exchange rate was slightly higher. Therefore, the market turned better after being weak in the morning. However, due to the national crisis, importers had no intention of doing business smoothly. Tianxiang telegrammed that 1,000 tons of small pressed rice would arrive in November at a price of 5 taels and 6 qian, but no large syndicates bought it in large quantities. The asking price for the returned goods in September was still low for small pressed rice, at 5 taels and 6 qian to 5 taels and 5 qian and 7 fen, totaling 300 tons. 100 tons of small pressed rice in October were priced at 5 taels and 6 qian and 8 fen, which was 8 fen higher for larger rice. The spot price for small pressed rice was 300 packages, priced at 12 yuan and 1 jiao, and Hunan Yuan rice was 287 packages, priced at 14 yuan.

Flour Market In A Drifting State

Yesterday's flour market saw a rise in the price of foreign wheat at the opening, with certain factories and outside buyers exhibiting strong buying interest. Prices rose consistently across all months, increasing by 1.5 fen to 0.5 fen compared to the previous day's close. The market sentiment was very positive, suggesting a continued upward trend. However, after the price increase, small and medium-sized factories, as well as many large speculators, seized the opportunity to sell, causing the market to level off again. Yet, before the close, large factories made purchases, resulting in another price reversal. The closing prices showed a 0.5 li increase for the current month, a 5 fen increase for October, and a 1 fen increase across November to February.

Wheat Rises in the Morning, Returns in the Afternoon

Yesterday, after the morning opening, prices for near and distant months of wheat rose in tandem. This was due to new and outside long positions in the distant months, and rumors of Hangzhou and Shaoxing buyers taking delivery of 200 carloads in the near months. The price of foreign wheat also rose by 1 or 2 jiao, leading to positive market sentiment and increases of around 5 fen across all months. Before the afternoon close, Runde and other firms newly arrived with a ship of foreign wheat and actively sold it into the market, particularly focusing on the current month. This resulted in an immediate drop in the current month, with other months also softening. The closing prices showed a decrease of 1 fen for the current month, an increase of 1 fen for October, an increase of 3 fen for November, and increases of 2 fen for December and January, with February up by 4 fen.

Northern and Southern Goods: The Downtrend of Honey Dates is Set

Honey dates have been slightly scarce in recent deliveries. However, the existing stock on the market is considered sufficient, and sales from various parties continue to be processed. As such, the market image is gradually stabilizing. Yesterday, the top-grade Hui-made "tu-tu" dates sold for 29 taels, and Lanxi "tu-tu" dates sold for 25 taels. Silk and Tea: Autumn Silkworm Cocoon Harvest in Changzhou and Wuxi Difficult to Abound

Unified Pull is No More Than Four Tenths of a Normal Year

Changzhou and Wuxi have long been known as prominent silkworm farming regions. Each year, the autumn silkworm quota is generally more abundant than in other counties. Although the silkworm egg supply was strong this year, the early silkworms suffered damage from continuous rain, and the late silkworms faced a major crisis of leaf scarcity due to the mulberry trees being submerged by water. Most of the silkworms in the strong leaf supply starved to death. Even those who managed to spin cocoons generally climbed the mountains hungry, with insufficient leaf consumption and thin, inferior cocoons. This year, the cocoon production in Changzhou and Wuxi is unified at no more than four tenths of a normal year.

Autumn Silkworm Pull Price in Zhejiang Not Cheap

In the cocoon regions of Hangzhou and Shaoxing in Zhejiang, although the autumn silkworm egg supply was not weak this year, the rainfall caused problems, and the cocoon production was still poor, unified at no more than three tenths of a normal year. The cocoon firms have been weighing and receiving for over ten days, and the amounts received have been very limited. Cocoon prices are not cheap because there are few goods and many firms, leading to competition for purchases. The average cocoon price in Hangzhou and Shaoxing is at least 62 or 63 yuan, and the cocoons are still of good quality. The cocoon market is gradually coming to an end.

Hardware Prices Rise Due to Sterling's Increase

Due to rumors of the British government suspending the gold standard, the British exchange rate has risen sharply in recent days, and the sterling rate in this port has also increased accordingly. As such, hardware merchants in this port who have not yet settled their exchange bills are all delighted. However, the prices of hardware from overseas have suddenly soared at this time. The market prices of copper, tin, and lead have all risen significantly and extraordinarily. Although transactions are not numerous, the sentiment is very strong. The Selling Price of Unprocessed Biji (Wool Fabric) Rises Sharply

Woolen goods and fabrics are currently in their prime selling season. Unprocessed, navy blue, gray, and miscellaneous colored biji are particularly popular. Local merchants are actively seeking to purchase them. The most popular color is the raw blue color. They are generally willing to trade if paired with other colors. Those who want to exclusively purchase the raw color are willing to add several fen of silver per yard because the inventory on the market is extremely scarce. Even those who purchase whole boxes are only allowed to pair two or three bolts. As such, there are sometimes three different price points. For example, the same brand of biji, paired with bare raw color, must be sold for 3 taels and 6 qian and a half, two yuan two sui two blue 2 taels and 6 qian, and bare gray color is sold for a reduced price of 2 taels and 5 qian and a half.

Coal: Changxing Coal Demand Exceeds Supply

After the Changxing Coal Mine started producing coal, the coal usage in the surrounding areas was supplied by this mine. Due to convenient transportation and low prices, the demand exceeds the supply. This year, in response to the needs of Shanghai, it has been sold in Shanghai, exclusively by the Yitai Hing Coal Company in this port. This coal is very suitable for the fuel of factory kilns, and the price is also low. Currently, the market price for Changxing blocks is 11 taels and a half, Changxing Unified is 8 taels and 7 qian and a half, Guangxing is 12 taels and a half, and Guangxing Selected is 9 taels and 7 qian and a half.

The Municipal Executive Committee

Sent Two Important Telegrams Yesterday

Please Vice-Zhang to Actively Prepare for War

Please Guangdong to Join Forces to Resist Foreign Aggression

The Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department received a telegram from Vice Commander Zhang, reporting the continued occupation of Yingkou, Andong, Changchun, and other places by the Japanese army. They immediately telegraphed back to Zhang yesterday, requesting him to order war preparations and announce the important documents submitted by the Japanese side. They also telegraphed the responsible persons in Guangdong, asking them to abandon their past grievances and join forces to resist foreign aggression. Each telegram is recorded separately below.

Telegram from Vice-Zhang (Abridged Title)

The entire process of the Japanese army's occupation of Shenyang has been reported in the Hao Day telecomunication. Based on reliable reports, the Japanese army has taken similar actions in Yingkou, Andong, Changchun, and other places. Andong was occupied at 6 a.m. on Qiao Chen, and Yingkou and Changchun were occupied at 8 a.m. on Hao Chen. The Chinese military police and armed forces in each city were disarmed. Detailed information is still being gathered by secret agents. Respectfully reported, Zhang Xueliang Hao, You.

Telegram to Vice-Zhang (Most Urgent)

To Vice Commander Zhang Hanqing, Beiping. Your telegram has been respectfully noted. Disregarding international law and destroying East Asian peace, the Japanese army took advantage of our natural disasters and banditry, suddenly sending troops to the Northeast, forcibly occupying Liaoning and Jilin, and invading Pingjin. The alarming news has aroused indignation. This extraordinary event is not only related to the survival of our country, but also destroys public law. The people of this city are filled with righteous indignation, feeling the pain as if it were their own. They are willing to make a firm determination to fight a protracted struggle. In addition to telegraphing the central government to quickly transfer troops to recover lost territory and consolidate national defense, and telegraphing Guangdong to abandon their past grievances and jointly face national difficulties, we urge you to order your troops to actively prepare for war, and not to retreat again, bringing shame to our country. Also, publicly announce the important documents submitted by the Japanese side, so that the whole world may know the truth of the matter. The comrades and compatriots of this city are filled with boiling blood and are willing to be the government's backing. This is a special reply to the telegram. Please consider it carefully. Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee.

Telegram to Guangdong

To Mr. Gu Xiangqin in Guangzhou, for all comrades. Japan has been plotting to invade our country for more than a day. They will proceed from occupying the Northeast to the Central Plains. This time, they took advantage of our natural disasters and banditry, suddenly sending troops, forcibly occupying Liaoning and Jilin, and invading Pingjin. Wherever the enemy's atmosphere reaches, the people are killed, their homes are burned, our military and civilian officials are captured, and our barracks and factories are seized. Public reason is treated as trash, human life is treated as grass, and the savagery is like madness. The alarming news has come, and all those with blood and breath, who can tolerate it? At this time, with national difficulties before us, at a critical moment, if we do not use the united strength of the whole country to take action to resist foreign insults, then there will be no intact eggs under the overturned nest. Since all comrades claim to be of the same party and country, how can there be more contention at this

Reader's Correspondence: Mr. Shen Tianbao's Message (Opposing Non-Resistance Against Japan)

Reports state that the Japanese are invading eastern provinces, committing extreme atrocities. Anyone with a sense of honor cannot help but be enraged. It has been three days since the incident occurred, yet no effective measures have been heard from the authorities in the eastern provinces. Instead, they have adopted a policy of non-resistance, the purpose of which is truly unknown. If they believe that now is not the time to contend with the Japanese, then when the ancestral tombs are dug up and houses are destroyed, when will they resist? If the Chinese army is currently unable to resist the Japanese, then in this critical time of survival, resistance may lead to destruction, but non-resistance also leads to destruction. Rather than passively waiting for death, wouldn't it be better to fight with a do-or-die spirit? If it is feared that resistance will provoke international disputes and complicate diplomatic relations, then if others unjustly attack us, we will respond with legitimate self-defense. What is wrong with that? Why give other countries an excuse for criticism? Alas, when Jinyang falls, they ask about hunting grounds, and when the Western Capital is destroyed, they ask who will be beheaded. When enemy soldiers arrive in force, they dare not even shoot a single arrow. This is like wild beasts worshiping hunters and begging for mercy. Is that possible? Your newspaper has always been a guide for society and a voice for the people. We hope for a response in the newspaper.

(Reply) A policy of non-resistance is something that those without strength or courage are forced to adopt. How can a grand nation with political and military power resort to this? If one province is occupied and there is no resistance, and then ten provinces are occupied and there is still no resistance, wouldn't that be the end? Alas, we firmly believe that the authorities will not willingly adopt a policy of non-resistance. However, before resisting, there must be various preparations. Exactly how to resist, who should resist, and with what should they resist are all problems. What we lament is not the current non-resistance, but the lack of preparation for resistance in ordinary times. As current citizens, we have no other choice but to urge everyone to quickly rise up. Please read yesterday's column in response to Mr. Shen Genghui's message. If you think it is correct, everyone should make a firm determination to act.

Revenue Stamp Notice: Municipal Government Inquires to Jiangsu Provincial Government to Lift Grain Ban in Liyang

The municipal government, based on a report submitted by the Social Affairs Bureau, stated that the Liyang County government's ban on grain exports was affecting the city's food supply. It immediately sent a telegram to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, ordering the county to lift the ban. It is expected that normal circulation will resume soon, ensuring that the city's grain supply is not affected.

Arsenal Experiences Second Fire

The Shanghai Arsenal in Gaochangmiao experienced a fire at 3:10 AM yesterday morning. The fire broke out unexpectedly in the gun factory behind the arsenal's office building. The fire blazed fiercely. Fire engines from various parts of southern Shanghai rushed to the scene upon receiving the news. However, due to the late hour and the area being a military stronghold, they were unable to enter. Later, the arsenal's security team investigated and allowed them to enter for firefighting. Three buildings and approximately 600 yuan worth of timber stored inside were burned down. The fire was extinguished by dawn. Fortunately, the machinery factory was not affected. Yesterday, the arsenal's director, Mr. Guo Chengen, stated that a fire had occurred in the artillery factory just over ten days ago. This was the second fire. An investigation revealed that the factory only had workers during the day and no one stayed overnight. Given the late hour, even if there were lingering embers, they should not have been delayed for so long before igniting. The sudden fire, occurring twice in such a short period, is particularly strange. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, he summoned the directors of the gun and artillery factories, as well as Mr. Wu Shihong, the head of the inspection department, to the North Station for discussions. On one hand, he instructed the arsenal's security team to conduct a thorough investigation, fearing that saboteurs were hiding within. Therefore, since the night before last, all security measures within Gaochangmiao have been tightened compared to the past.

Yingkou Customs Salt Tax Returned

It was previously reported that the Yingkou Customs salt tax was seized by the Japanese army. The Bank of China received a telegram from its Dalian branch yesterday, reporting that the customs salt tax had been fully returned by the Japanese army and was still being managed by the receiving bank.

Tanaka's Conspiracy to Annex Manchuria and Mongolia

The China Review Weekly is the best English newspaper run by Chinese people and serves as a voice for the Chinese people to the outside world. It has been published for four years. Recently, due to Japan's military aggression in the Northeast, the entire country is filled with anger. At this critical moment of survival, it is necessary to widely publicize the urgency of the national salvation movement, to inform the friendly countries the brutal truth about the Japanese. It has published a special issue on Japanese invasion, with very rich content, and includes the full text of the "Tanaka Memorial," which everyone should read. Each copy is still sold for two dimes, and the annual subscription is seven yuan. Overseas Chinese from Mexico to Arrive in Shanghai

The expulsion of Chinese from Mexico is unbearable. The first group of overseas Chinese returning from Mexico, totaling 184 people, has sailed from Mexico to New York, and then transferred to the President Monroe of the Dollar Steamship Line to Shanghai. Yesterday, a telegram was received in Shanghai stating that the overseas Chinese had arrived in Kobe, Japan. Upon hearing about the Japanese invasion of their homeland and the loss of the eastern provinces, they were all filled with grief and indignation. As a result, they stayed on the ship and did not disembark. They have now left Japan on the original ship and are expected to arrive in Shanghai next Monday (the 28th) morning. The ship is expected to enter the port before 8:00 AM and proceed to the Bailianjing Wharf in Pudong, where the overseas Chinese will transfer to small steamships to disembark at the Customs Wharf. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai around 9:00 AM.

Li Zuchao Discusses Ideas for Developing Fisheries

Li Zuchao, Chief of the Fisheries Section of the Fisheries Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Industry for the Jiangzhe Region, said yesterday that the scope of fisheries can be broadly divided into three categories: fishing, aquaculture, and manufacturing. For improvement, experimentation is essential. For experimentation, investigation comes first. It is the duty of this bureau to dispatch specialists to the coastal islands of Jiangsu and Zhejiang and the Shanghai urban area for separate investigations. However, those involved in fisheries are generally suspicious and secretive, which is a major obstacle. The main reason is that fishermen have limited knowledge and rarely interact with government offices, leading to this situation. Therefore, promoting fisheries education is a fundamental priority. I (Mr. Li referring to himself) plan to suggest that the education authorities issue a circular to all coastal counties, either establishing fisheries primary schools in each fishing area or adding aquatic product knowledge to the curriculum of each primary school. At the same time, the fisheries administrative organs should provide guidance from the sidelines. This coordinated approach will achieve twice the results with half the effort. As for short-term measures, we are actively planning to establish manufacturing plants, conduct aquaculture trials, purchase fishing vessels and gear, explore new fishing grounds, and promote new technologies. This bureau has selected a section of the Gongtu outside Wangongtang in Zhenhai County, Zhejiang, to prepare for shellfish cultivation trials. We will soon submit a request to the Ministry of Industry to allocate funds for phased implementation. However, funding is the mother of all undertakings, and even more so for groundbreaking initiatives. Whether we can achieve our goals depends entirely on the funding allocated by the Ministry. Furthermore, there is something I must say: Chinese fishermen generally lack a long-term vision. When a new fishing ground is discovered or a new technology is invented, they often keep it secret. Even worse, unscrupulous fish merchants are willing to act as accomplices, trading foreign fish. The lack of unity among fishermen and fish merchants has led to a decline in the fisheries market. It is truly heartbreaking to speak of. The key to recovery lies in collective effort, open cooperation between government and the people. The future of fisheries may then have hope for development. However, public awareness through promotion and advocacy is what we hope the media will provide with full support.

British Public Buses Almost Fully Recovered

Striking Workers Re-Petition

After the British public bus workers went on strike again, the company refused to reinstate them and the authorities rejected their demands. The striking workers are in a state of unemployment. The Route 3 and Route 6 public buses resumed service the day before yesterday. Yesterday, the workers went to the Social Affairs Bureau again to petition. However, the company, based on a board resolution, refused to reinstate the striking workers and negotiate conditions, and instead hired new workers to restore traffic on all routes. Later, because Route 3 from Zhoujiaqiao to Caonongdu and Route 6 from Tilanqiao to Gongyuan Bazichang are located in remote areas, it was feared that accidents might occur, so service was temporarily suspended. Recently, seeing that the striking workers have taken no action, service was restored from the day before yesterday.

The Western food industry's treatment conditions have been fully negotiated through repeated mediation by the Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Party Headquarters, which jointly convened a labor-management conciliation committee. Wu Shenxiang and Zhao Jinghua of the Western Food Industry Union attended on time. Lin Zhenchuan and Wu Furen of the Western Food Industry Association were absent. Emergency Hospital for Epidemic Diseases Extends Treatment Period

Extended to October 15th

After the flood, the cholera epidemic spread rapidly. Some of the epidemic hospitals and the epidemic departments attached to other hospitals have already closed, but the epidemic has been increasing recently, causing overcrowding in the hospitals that have not closed. The Emergency Hospital for Epidemic Diseases on North Xizang Road usually closes at the end of September each year. However, a letter was received from the Bureau of Health stating that the cholera epidemic this year is more severe than in previous years, and it may not be completely eliminated until mid-October. Patients with the disease must have a corresponding treatment facility. It has recently been learned that some of the epidemic hospitals and the epidemic departments attached to other hospitals in the city have already closed or are about to close, which means that later patients will have no place to be treated. Please ensure that your hospital adheres to its original purpose and extends the treatment period to October 15th. Do not stop treating cholera patients before the epidemic is completely eliminated. This matter concerns public health and requires your cooperation. After receiving the letter, the hospital immediately convened an emergency medical meeting. Considering the severity of the current epidemic and the large number of disaster victims, if there is no corresponding treatment facility, not only will poor patients have nowhere to be treated, but the epidemic will also spread, which is a major concern. Therefore, it was unanimously decided to follow the instructions in the letter from the Bureau of Health and extend the treatment of cholera patients to October 15th to benefit the patients. All expenses exceeding the budget will be actively raised by the directors.

Police Arrest Six Kidnappers

Rescued Six Kidnapped Children

At approximately 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, detectives He Xiaozhi, Zhang Shipin, and Wang Youshan of the Hongkou Police Department learned that kidnappers were hiding at No. 305 Kunming Road. They secretly went to the address with foreign detective Sauer and arrested Chen Zhang, a woman from Anhui. They found a kidnapped child named Akang (7 years old), who lived at a certain address in Yuanyuli, Yangshupu, and another child named Xu Baohe (10 years old) from Nanjing. Under interrogation, they learned that there were accomplices at No. 545 of the same road. The detectives went there and arrested Wang Huanan and Wang Lichun from Anhui, Chen Xianren (also known as Chen Zhang's husband), and Yang Wanchun from Henan. They also found a kidnapped boy named Wang Xinlin (9 years old) from Nanjing and a boy from Zhenjiang named Shi Xiaoxizi (14 years old). They then went to No. 543 Meizhou Road and arrested another accomplice, Zhao Duan, a woman from Anhui. In this operation, a total of six kidnappers were arrested and four children were rescued. All were taken back to the police station and detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. According to the police lawyer Qian Xunjiu, the case involved family members of the children who were in Nanjing and Zhenjiang, and some were local but could not be found. Therefore, none of them were present in court today, and a postponement was requested. Detective He and others then reported the circumstances of the arrest of the defendants. According to the child Shi Xiaoxizi, he was from Zhenjiang and lived in Shuimahe near the city in his hometown. His mother washed clothes to make a living. He went out to collect scraps every day. Five or six days ago, he was lured to Nanjing Railway Station by the defendant Wang Huanan and came to Shanghai with the defendants Wang Lichun and Yang Wanchun. According to the child Wang Xinlin, he was from Nanjing but did not know where he lived. He had no father but had a mother and uncle who had gone back to their hometown. The child spoke fluent Shanghai dialect but knew nothing else. According to the child Akang, he lived in Yuanyu, Shanghai, but did not know the address. He had both parents, his father's name was Afa, and he was previously with Chen Zhang through Uncle Jia. He knew nothing else. After Judge Xiao Xiehuan questioned the defendants, their answers were evasive. He ordered them to be detained separately for further interrogation at a later date. The four children, including Shi Xiaoxizi, were temporarily sent to the Women and Children Relief Society for care.

Indian Beats Poor Girl to Death by Drowning

See How to Seek Justice

Xu Xiaomei, a ten-year-old girl from Shandong, recently had difficulty making a living due to poverty. Therefore, her father, Xu Jinzhong, taught her to play with a small knife, using a small sickle used by farmers to cut rice. She would throw it up and down on three sides and carry a small drum or gong to beg for money from shops and residents along the streets of Shanghai to supplement the family income. At around 10:00 AM on the 19th of this month, Xu was again playing with a knife and begging for money from the public at the North Bund Wharf of the China Merchants Bureau in Hongkou. An Indian watchman named Kataxing came forward to beat her away. Xu tried to escape to the riverbank. The Indian continued to chase her relentlessly, causing Xu to have nowhere to escape and being forced to the riverbank. She tried to jump onto a sampan boat parked there, but the sampan was a little far from the shore. The girl was weak and lost her footing, falling into the river. Passersby Cai Jinshan and Wang Yushan saw this and immediately reported it to the River Patrol Police. Efforts to rescue her were unsuccessful. It was not until the day before yesterday that the body was recovered. The Huishan Police took the body to the Fei Lun Road autopsy center. Yesterday, Inspector Guo of the First District Court of the Special Court arrived at the center to examine the body. He then presided over a public hearing. Xu Jinzhong, the girl's father, filed a case requesting justice. The Indian, Kataxing, stated that because the Dalai ship was about to set sail, he saw many people disembarking from sampans on the floating bridge, so he drove the girl away. Witnesses Cai Jinshan and Wang Yushan testified one after another that they saw the Indian beating Xu and chasing her. The judge ruled that it was proven that the girl was chased by the Indian and fell into the river and drowned. The body was handed over to Xu Jinzhong for coffining and temporary burial, pending further investigation.

Youth Garden: School Opens - Xi

The rustling autumn wind brings coolness. In the blink of an eye, it is the beginning of the school year again. Students are all happily carrying their books to school, preparing for the work of attending classes. The schools, which have been temporarily quiet for more than two months, have suddenly become bustling markets again. Their hearts are filled with a kind of joyful color, as if these youthful lives have no sorrow. Even if there have been attacks and wounds, they have been healed at this moment. Their hearts are only thinking about how they will spend this living salt of life's consciousness.

Yes, they will not know what worry is. The word "worry" will never impress them.

Today, according to the school's notices, school has opened. So I got up very early to be on time for school. But when I got there, I couldn't help but doubt my eyes. Why were there so few people? Later, I asked a janitor and learned that today was only the opening ceremony, and there were no classes yet. Moreover, the opening ceremony had to wait until 11:00 AM. Disappointed, I casually walked to the letter rack to see if there were any letters. There happened to be one, and judging from the handwriting, I immediately knew it was from fellow student Fang. It was written simply:

Senior XX, I have been feeling extremely depressed lately, beyond imagination. If you have time, please come and talk to me to ease my loneliness.

Sincerely, XX. West Dormitory, third floor, Room 208, today. I felt that analyzing this letter, it seemed somewhat peculiar. Although it inevitably had a depressing meaning, perhaps he really had some real situation that was making him feel inexplicably down. That's what I thought at the time, so I walked to his room.

I pushed open the door, and fellow student Fang was still not up. A wave of odor rushed into my nostrils. I trembled and anxiously called out to him,

"Fellow student Fang, are you still not up? It's getting late."

He rubbed his sleepy eyes and looked at me with a kind of sluggish but grateful look. After a long while, he pieced together this sentence,

"Ah, it's really you. I just dreamed that you came. How coincidental."

Truly, on his thin face, his haggard expression of worry so clearly showed his depressed state. Only he lived in this room, and things were spread out in extreme disarray, as if the master of this place had not given them time to tidy up for a long time.

He still didn't get up, but I didn't feel that this was his arrogance. I only felt that this increased his decadence even more. At that time, because I was eager to know the reason for what was said in the letter, I didn't care that this would be a question that would hurt him when he heard it.

"Recently," I said, "what exactly is wrong with you?" When he heard my question, his breathing immediately became rapid.

"Friend," he said after a moment of silence, "this is fate. This is heaven making our family broken and destroyed. At this moment, I don't know where my parents, my brothers and sisters are wandering. Isn't this heaven destroying us?"

He was somewhat choked up. I couldn't figure it out for a moment, so I asked again,

"So, is the cause of this incident entirely attributed to heaven?"

"Yes, because I can't blame anyone else, I can only blame heaven. Since the summer vacation, because I wanted to attend summer school, I didn't go back. But soon I saw news in the newspaper about floods in my hometown. I couldn't help but be alarmed and quickly wrote an express letter to ask how things were at home. After about ten days, I received a reply saying that things were still okay, but after that, I never received another letter. And the news in the newspaper became more alarming every day. Alas, heaven, at this moment, I am a homeless wanderer wandering in a foreign land. What else am I hoping for?"

His voice was tragic and impassioned, as powerful as when he was speaking of national humiliation. It was then that I realized that my friend's hometown was in the disaster area.

"Friend," I said, comforting him with sympathy that I couldn't express in words, "This is indeed a fatal blow to you. However, this is still a matter of our entire nation's life. We have no power to save it. The only thing we can do now is to work hard ourselves and think about how to cultivate our knowledge and prepare to serve the country. If we become depressed again, who will the future country push onto to take care of it?"

He was silent.

Friend, we can only bear the pain for a moment. The future hope is concentrated on us. We bear so much responsibility," I couldn't help but get excited.

"..." But he still didn't say a word, as if he had some great hidden pain. Of course, people can't be without feelings, and in this environment, it is absolutely unavoidable. So I didn't say anything more. Only silent air circulated between us.

"Friend, let's bear the pain and work hard," I said, unable to bear the low pressure, and walked out in disappointment. Afterwards, I realized that this attitude was unfair to my friend.

The next evening, I received a letter from him delivered by the postman:

Senior XX, I am grateful for your comforting me this morning. In fact, you think, the situation at home has become so bad that even people with hearts of stone would have thoughts of hating the world. Moreover, I am being chased by life here and am constantly trapped in a state of helplessness, which only adds to my infinite grief and indignation. Since the aid from home has been cut off, the only way is to take money from the "son's home" (i.e., pawnshop) to use. But the things are limited, and soon they will all be pawned off. Up to now, I owe a lot to my friends, and I can't bring myself to borrow from them anymore. However, the school's opening notice is like a death warrant. I ask you, how can a penniless person have so much money? Even if the school can be lenient, I still have to pay at least some of it. And now, even the problem of eating is not settled, so everything else is just a dream. So, I thought about it a thousand times. Should I drop out of school? My stomach is empty, and in this commercialized society, what can I do? Should I continue to study? It's just a pipe dream of eating swan meat. What you advised me, how could I not know? Otherwise, I would have abandoned the world long ago. Friend, please save me. How should I dispose of my life? Yes, the faces of my classmates are all showing joyful smiles, but how much it stabs my marrow.

I couldn't bear to read it all, and I only felt a wave of darkness in front of my eyes.

Trying - Xi

Wei was forced to leave his hometown again, a young man who just turned eighteen this year. Due to the pressures of various environments, he had to embark on this dirty road to work hard. How sad this is.

About a month ago, he came to Shanghai to look for work. He happened to meet several of his friends from his hometown who were gathering in Shanghai to discuss how to run a newspaper back home. So they pushed him to take charge. After considering the results, because this career was very suitable for him, he agreed without hesitation. In less than five days, he abandoned his original wandering plan and returned to his hometown of low pressure.

After that, I didn't receive any news from him. Friends who cared about him all asked me, thinking that only I knew clearly. Little did they know that I was still trying my best to find out.

○○○

This was a clear morning when I was still in my dream. I suddenly heard a voice calling me. I quickly rubbed my sleepy eyes and recognized that it was Wei. At that time, I was very surprised how he could have the leisure to come to Shanghai. His face looked very pale, full of the haggard look of wind and dust. My heart was filled with indescribable sympathy. Alas, our society has actually trapped a lively young man under its violent authority.

"I have already broken up with them," he began to tell his story. "They are not human. I can't stand it no matter what." His tone was fierce with indignation.

"What?" I thought he had another conflict with his family. "Maybe you are..."

"The newspaper can't be run," he said, adding as if he didn't hear my question. And at this point I understood, "They want to use me as their puppet, to do that career with color, and put all the blame and responsibility on me. How can I cooperate with that?"

Indeed, Wei is a young man with strong principles. Although trapped in a depressed and poor situation, he would never be tempted by some small gains. His heart is pure and innocent. This deception was something he never expected. With his experience, he would not have expected his friends to be setting a trap for him.

"I was extremely angry after all," he continued, "When I discovered this background, I immediately broke away. They also repeatedly invited people to intercede, but I honestly refused. I felt that it was better to go outside. Even if I wander and live by selling my brainpower, it is much better than suffering that."

"So, you want to decide to do this? But you have to know that this unstable life may not give you a good place of production. Don't expect too much from this." I said in the tone that I had always used to persuade him. In fact, everyone understands that the suffering of this kind of labor is truly unspeakable. He only relies on his ideals to construct his pursuit. So I continued, "This is a dangerous road. It is difficult to try."

"But I am now in a position where I have to try. Other than this, what can give me work? My family really makes me feel suffocated, so I can't care about the problems after this. I resolutely came out. This time, I even brought my luggage..."

"Your spirit is commendable, but..."

A solemn silence occupied the defense line between you and me.

Finally, he said, "I want to rent a small room to live in and then talk about it. I have decided to develop my energy in literature."

"Okay, you try it on this journey. I will do my best to help you."
