Social News: Slump in Tin and Rubber Markets (Continued) - Qiu Bincun

The slump in tin and rubber markets and the wave of unemployment are not limited to Singapore and Penang, but are widespread in the Netherlands, England, Siam, France, America, and other places.

(III) Relief for the Slump in Tin and Rubber Markets

(A) For Capitalists: The main points are to restrict production and reduce inventory.

(I) Methods of Relief for Rubber

Rubber relief must be through the British Malaya government and the Dutch East Indies government to discuss the restrictions policy. The method can emulate the London Malaya Rubber industry, the board of directors of each company and other such organizations agree by telegram to order the companies to implement a reduction in cutting, in order to reduce production. The method of calculating the index of reduction is as follows:

Mariembi-Bikois Company Limited, 30% reduction

United Eastern Plantation Company, 30% reduction

Johore Central Rubber Estates, 30% reduction

Krajong Rubber Planting Company, 30% reduction

Malacca Alor Gajah Rubber Estates, 25% reduction

Federated Malay States Rubber Company, 35% reduction

(II) Methods of Relief for Tin

Mr. Rawlote, an official of the Federated Malay States Mines Department, invented the Rawlote New Policy. His proposal is to reduce current inventories so that the current low price of tin can be extended to a normal level. After the invention of this Rawlote New Policy, it was immediately proposed and discussed by British tin industrialists and Malayan tin industrialists for a considerable period, lasting several months. The result was that many judgments stated that if this new policy were put into practice, it would definitely achieve the purpose of relieving the tin industry. The conditions of this new policy are detailed below:

1. At least 30% of the world's tin producers, and 40% of tin producers from the Federated Malay States, Bolivia, Siam, and Nigeria, etc., guarantee that they will no longer mine tin, no matter what, in order for the price of tin to reach a turnaround price (200 pounds).

2. Those who agree with and are willing to implement this new policy should sell a portion of the unmined tin to large organized companies. The price will be based on the market price, plus 50% of the difference between the market price and the turnaround price, to the point where it can only maintain the current state of the tin mine.

3. The tin will be transacted, or the tin payment will be cleared, only after the turnaround price is reached.

4. Tin producers, etc., should organize a large company with sufficient capital of 1.5 million gold pounds to enable this policy to be realized.

The above four items are the conditions of the Rawlote New Policy. Fearing that there are still unclear points, a specific example is given below:

For example, a certain tin mine produces 1,000 piculs of tin per month. According to the current market price, it is calculated at 40 yuan per picul, which is 40,000 yuan. If the maintenance cost is 8,000 yuan, and the turnaround price is 200 pounds, that is, 60 yuan per picul. The tin produced is now sold to the newly organized large company at 40 yuan per picul (market price), plus 50% of the difference between the market price and the turnaround price (i.e., 60 yuan minus 40 yuan, which is 20 yuan, this is the difference, and then 50% of that is 10 yuan), giving 50 yuan per picul. If Tin Mine A sells 160 piculs per month, calculated at 50 yuan per picul, it can get 8,000 yuan, which is enough for expenses. And this tin mine's 1,000 piculs will not be mined for the time being until the turnaround price (200 pounds, i.e., 60 yuan per picul) is realized.

Tin mining companies have seen this. According to a Reuters London dispatch on December 26, 1930, "The Chairman of the Tin Producers' Association issued a notice to members outlining the international agreement plan for the balance of tin production. This agreement is currently under final consideration by the governments of the countries concerned. If they all agree, it can be implemented. The clauses are as follows: (1) The international quota must be calculated from January 1, 1931. All tin or tin ingots exported after the end of December must be counted in the quota for the first quarter of 1931. (2) This agreement should remain valid for the year. (3) The quota can be changed at any time according to the situation, because the purpose of this agreement is to adjust supply and demand and

A Few Small Patriotic Stories 102

— Young Yi

When Prussia was ravaged by Napoleon I, the national spirit was boosted. Women all took off their gold jewelry and exchanged it for iron because iron could strengthen the country. Germany has the saying "Iron is gold."

As a result of the Franco-Prussian War in 1870, France was defeated. The treaties under the siege were: (1) to cede the two provinces of Alsace and Lorraine; (2) to pay an indemnity of 5,000 million. This huge sum of 5,000 million was paid off by France in a few days because all the common people took out everything they had. Therefore, the German Prime Minister Bismarck sighed and said, "France will always be our big problem." An Italian poor and sick child was on a ship. A foreigner saw his pity and gave him some money. He was very grateful, but when the foreigner and another person talked about the failure of the Italian country, the child took out the money given to him and went to the foreigner. "I don't want money from people who scold my country."

Before the Russo-Japanese War, a Russian on a street in Japan saw a Japanese child and gave him some sweets to eat. As soon as the child saw that it was a Russian, he refused to accept his things, saying, "You are Russian, you can't have your food."

During the Russian Empire, the Crown Prince of Russia once toured Lake Biwa in Japan. Seeing the beautiful scenery, he proudly said, "When will my palace be built here?" His sycophantic subordinates said, "It's right in front of you." A Japanese police chief accompanying the Russian prince, after hearing this, took out the hand from his waist and shot at the Russian prince, but missed.

Compatriots, what do you think after reading these few short stories today when foreign troubles are imminent?

World Tidbits 103

A Special Mail: The most special and strange mail in the world was recently delivered to London by the post office. This mail was a very large package, a living package. This package was Belgian journalist G. Lantcheere. He paid the postage in the Brussels Post Office and sent it to a certain place in London as a sample of something worthless. At that time, the post office attached a label and stamped it with a postmark. It was sent directly to London in the aircraft's parcel compartment. When the plane landed in Croydon, the staff of the British Post Office checked and delivered it. He came all the way, and there was not much difference from other passengers, but he was in the parcel compartment and had no chair to sit on, because a parcel certainly does not need a chair. In terms of cost, the fare for an ordinary passenger to fly from Brussels to London by plane is four pounds, while the postage for this living package is only two pounds and eight pence. However, when he returns to Belgium, he can no longer use this method, because the British Post Office does not accept such living packages sent abroad. If it is within the territory of the United Kingdom, then whether it is sent as a parcel or as an express letter, it can be handled.

Precious Scraps from Overseas 104

— Yi Mei

Land is a world, and the sea is also a world. Sea creatures, the most ferocious and giant ones, such as whales, seals, manatees, sea tigers, and sea elephants, etc. We can see them in aquariums or on the screen. According to Spanish scientist Limbrech Clock, the sea is immeasurably deep, and there are probably tens of millions of species of creatures. However, sunlight only reaches 600 feet below the surface of the water, and no human has ever dived to 6,000 feet or more. The creatures seen in aquariums and on the screen are only one-tenth or one-twelfth of the total. The creatures below 6,000 feet are strange and indescribable, and all the creatures have no eyes, because sunlight does not reach them, and the eyes are eliminated and lose their effectiveness. Although this comes from Limbrech Clock's speculation, the principle may be true.

The big bananas in Siam are about a foot long and unusually large. Eating one can make people full, so getting two or three bananas a day is enough to eat and be happy, drumming their bellies and enjoying themselves. It is not more than the people of Huxley.

The Eagle Yang is also called the Mexican Yang, which is the national currency of Mexico. On the obverse of the coin is an eagle with a snake in its beak. What is the purpose of this? Few people know it. Some say that in the past, the Mexican revolution failed. A certain revolutionary leader fled to a barren valley. One day, he saw a small eagle fighting a giant snake. The eagle exhausted all its strength and killed the snake and pecked it to pieces. The revolutionary leader was greatly inspired, fed his horses, sharpened his weapons, and reorganized his troops. In one fell swoop, the revolution was completed. Once the foundation was laid, coins were cast to depict eagles and snakes, so as not to forget their encouraging contribution. I don't know if the statement is credible.

Research on Planting American Wheat 105

— Pan Zhiben

After reading Mr. Chen Yangnian's research on American wheat varieties published in "Free Talk" on September 20, I couldn't help but feel terrified. This year's rice has failed to produce any grains, and we must rely on foreign food for maintenance. If we plant miscellaneous grains with little certainty after the disaster, we will still have to beg for foreign food next spring. Therefore, the miscellaneous grains planted this winter must be ones that are fully certain and can be harvested. Do not rashly try to plant American wheat and treat people's lives as a game. Therefore, Dr. Love solemnly declared: Misplanting American wheat will be unimaginable. Now I will describe it one by one on the left.

(1) American wheat includes all the remaining wheat in the United States. Due to different climates, different soils, and different amounts of rainfall, some grow in the southern United States and are not suitable for the north, and some grow in the north and may not be suitable for the east. This is the case in its own country, let alone transplanted to our country.

(2) American wheat includes a large number of varieties. Some varieties are suitable for a certain place in our country, while others are not suitable for a certain place. It is not easy to know whether they are suitable or not until after trial planting. According to Mr. Chen, the American wheat he has planted in the past ten years has achieved very good results. I am afraid that the American wheat Mr. Chen planted is suitable for the soil and climate of Jiangzhou, Zhenjiang. But I don't know what the scientific name of the American wheat Mr. Chen planted is. Can you tell me? It can also be an aid to the experiment.

(3) I also sent Jinling University No. 26 improved wheat to my home in Ninghai, Zhejiang, for trial planting. The results were equal to zero. It may be due to unsuitable soil, climate, or rainfall, resulting in short and unfruitful stems. According to the research, No. 26 wheat is a native wheat near Nanjing, not a foreign product. It is not suitable for its own country, let alone American wheat.

(4) The government and local authorities set up agricultural experiment fields to introduce good varieties from other countries and improve the original varieties of our country. After testing them and confirming their effectiveness, they then advise farmers to plant them.

Records of What I Saw and Heard in the Old Capital 106

— Zhu An

In the early years of Jiaqing, Japan had an engraving of "A Collection of Famous Landscape Pictures of Tang Dynasty". This book has been widely circulated recently. It is all works of tracing and imitating by those who traveled to the capital and returned to their country at that time. The order of its volumes is: first the Inner Court, then the Imperial City, then the Inner City, then the Outer City, then the surrounding gardens and suburbs, and finally the various prefectures of Zhili. Its compilation starts with a general map and then goes on to the norms, cultural relics, scenery and famous places, followed by explanations, and references to inscriptions by famous people. For the Inner Court, there are pictures of emperors and empresses wearing winter and summer court clothes, pictures of morning visits at the Meridian Gate, pictures of the nine gates inside the Meridian Gate, pictures of the grand court meeting at the Hall of Supreme Harmony, pictures of banquets for foreign Mongolian vassals at the Hall of Preserving Harmony on New Year's Eve, and pictures of small banquets at the Palace of Chonghua. For the Imperial City, there are pictures of proclamations being issued at Tiananmen Square, pictures of peony and peony flowers being offered on the Lantern Festival, pictures of ice games, pictures of martial arts examination for Jinshi at the Ziguang Pavilion, and pictures of the emperor plowing the fields and the empress raising silkworms. All of these are the prosperity of fame and cultural relics in the era of peace, which cannot be fully seen even in books such as "Collection of Statutes". As for the pictures of the East and West Peace Gates, the pictures of the four memorial archways, and the pictures of the Zhengyang Gate and Zhengyang Bridge, they are the traces of the city streets in the capital, which can be used to verify the ancient from the present and are like matching talismans. As for the various government offices, temples, altars, gardens and imperial residences, either their names remain, or their locations have been obliterated. Looking at their paintings, they all appear as if they can be seen. The efforts of construction and creation over hundreds of years can still exist in our imagination for a long time. This is indeed a rare treasure of illustrated books that has not been seen in China. As for the system of figures and clothing, most of them are far from the current situation. Those who love the ancient are especially indispensable to take a look. I think that the most interesting thing about the changes in customs from ancient to modern times is the offering building and the brothel. The pictures of the East and West Qinglou recorded are in the area east of today's Dengshikou. The prostitutes are all dressed in long robes and heavy makeup, playing the zither and pipa to entertain the wine. The embroidered curtains and red candles are far from what can be seen in today's world. The stage of the Zha Building outside Zhengyang Gate is not different from the current system. However, all the spectators are standing in the open. Women began to live in mat sheds. In the old-fashioned theaters before the Republic of China, the seats were all arranged in long benches, and if you listened with your ears, you would not face the stage directly. Women lived upstairs. If men and women sat together, it would be greatly criticized by the current public opinion, and the police station would strictly prohibit it. Therefore, it is known that it is a relic of the Qianlong and Jiaqing eras. Now, there are only a few of these theaters left. Men and women sit together, and no one dares not to obey. The painting base of the "Collection of Famous Landscape Pictures of Tang Dynasty" is very thought-provoking. The words "Guanghe Zha Building" are written on the memorial archway. The Zha Building was created by a wealthy merchant surnamed Zha. Therefore, all theaters are named after Zha. I don't know when it was mistakenly called "Tea". Only by obtaining this book can we correct the misunderstanding of the people of the capital that has been passed down for generations.

According to Mr. Chen's statement, if a person obtains excellent results in trying a crop in one place, he thinks it is okay. Then why does the government spend huge amounts of money to run agricultural experiment fields?

(5) Mr. Chen said, "The earlier American wheat is planted, the better." I don't know that early is enough to kill it. Wheat has a dormancy period to protect it from the cold. It starts to germinate and grow after the spring warms up. If it germinates too early, it will easily be frozen to death. American farmers put cattle and horses into wheat fields in winter or use stone rollers to press it to prevent it from growing too vigorously. This is why.

I think that at this critical moment of life and death, there should be no remarks to show off. "I don't know what the doctor based his claim on." If the limelight comes out, the ignorant will echo it, and then tens of millions of lives will be in danger. (Moved to help with disaster relief)

Strange Records 107

— Zheng Yanfan

The theory of astrology has been around for a long time. Because I think it is close to superstition and occasionally a coincidence, I have never dared to believe it. Thinking about it now, I realize that the reason why it has been passed down for so long and has not declined is because there is a reason for it.

The evening before yesterday, I accepted an invitation from a relative and friend to a banquet at his house. Before the banquet was half over, a servant hurriedly brought a telegram, saying that my father was seriously ill. My elder brother sent a telegram to urge me to return home. The whole table was shocked. I immediately planned to return home and set off overnight. My friend said, "It's too late. Why don't you wait until tomorrow? Fortunately, Mr. Liang is here, you can consult him. He should be able to tell you whether it's a bad omen or a good omen." Although I didn't believe my friend's words, I was in a state of confusion and could no longer control myself. The gentleman looked at me for a long time and asked my age. My friend told him one by one. After a while, the gentleman smiled and said to me, "Your father's illness is not mild. It starts with chills and fever, and then diarrhea. But a lucky person will be blessed by God. He will be able to turn danger into safety. Good news will arrive in no more than three days. You don't have to go. It's just a waste of time to go back and forth." I listened to his words and thought that Mr. Liang saw people's misfortune and deliberately made comforting words to relieve it. Moreover, my old father is nearly seventy years old and his body is weak. If he is not seriously ill, he will never send an urgent telegram to urge me to return home. I still didn't believe it. Before the banquet was over, I said goodbye and went home. So I prepared everything and bought a ticket to return south. When I arrived home, my father's illness was indeed cured and he ate as usual. Suddenly I met Mr. Liang and asked him about the illness in surprise. My father told him about it and said, "I sent you a fast mail yesterday to ask you not to come back." At this point, I had to believe what I had never dared to believe before. Mr. Liang is thousands of miles away from my hometown. How could he know the beginning of the illness? How could he know the condition of the illness? He was able to know that the illness was not a problem. And he said, "There will be good news in no more than three days." Indeed, everything was as he said. The mystery in this is unknowable. The gentleman's name is Zuo Shu, and his other name is Zhen Zuo Bi. He was born lame and had a right wrist. He only relies on his left hand to write. He is a strange person in Guangdong. He used to set up a writing desk in Central, Hong Kong, and was famous for a while. He is now living at 162 North Sichuan Road. I will go to thank him when I have the chance. (Decline the reward)

Fiction Helping Wheel Association

A Husband's Wife (22) 108

— Jiang Hongjiao

"This can't be considered a debate. Maybe there are fewer people in your family, and there are fewer troubles that occur in the family, at least you have fewer things to worry about than I do. Auntie there, I have to subsidize her twenty yuan every month. She has no children. It's really hard. An old aunt, although she lives in her nephew's house, her nephew's situation is not good either, and I subsidize her ten yuan every month. My wife is younger than you, but we got married earlier and have had this big bunch of children. The education expenses every year have accounted for 30% of my income. I have also sent the two youngest to nursery schools. I really can't bear it. These two children have mothers, but no one pays attention to their clothing, food, and shelter. They are only controlled by servants, so I don't want them to live at home. You think my monthly expenses are not very large, right? But my wife is still not satisfied with the money I provide her. She is always complaining about being poor every day. One minute she has no money to pick up the custom-made leather shoes, the next minute she is clamoring that she has no money to pay for the vegetable bill for entertaining guests, and the next minute she is planning how to pay for the club membership fee. The purchase of other decorations and the consumption of going to movies and dance halls really make me exhausted and difficult to supply, so I feel that the deterioration of the relationship between husband and wife is mostly caused by money. What do you say?" Mr. Chen was half complaining and half trying to tell Mrs. Li about his financial situation, hoping that she could suggest some ways to manage his finances.

"How is the money for your household expenses distributed to your wife every month?" Mrs. Li was ready to contribute some advice.

"It would be great if you could tell me how to save money. I know my own faults, which is that I don't have an accurate budget, so I have accumulated a large deficit: but in good conscience, I use very little money myself."

"You should stipulate an amount, accurately give your wife the amount for household expenses and the amount to supply her, and agree with her that she is not allowed to exceed it, or it may make your finances a little less."

"Alas! If I did that, she would definitely transfer the household expenses to other uses and spend it all on herself: as a result, there would be no household expenses, and I would have to find a way to pay for it a second time."

"Then from now on, you will manage all the household expenses yourself, and you will only give her a personal monthly allowance. Don't give her too much. Isn't that also a standard?"

"I'm busy enough with work outside during the day, and I still have to manage the household. Why do I need a wife?"

Gold Prices Continue to Plunge Violently 109

Drop of...Seventeen Taels

Fluctuation Range Still Extremely Wide

Plus Special Margin of Fifteen Taels

Conflicting News, Treacherous Situation: Yesterday's Spot Gold Still Had Extremely Fierce Fluctuations, With Tumultuous Waves and Utter Horror. However, The Downward Trend Intensified, With An Initial Drop of Over Ten Taels, Which Was Irresistible. People's Hearts Were Extremely Distracted, and Nothing Could Be Done. The Difference Between The Morning and Afternoon Markets Was Nearly Forty Taels. In The End, It Continued to Fall Seventeen Taels. There Was Quite A Bit of Confusion in The Market. The Silver Market's Rise and Fall Was Quite Different. British Gold Rose While American Gold Fell. Therefore, It Opened Slightly Lower, Then Turned Weak to Strong, Once Exceeding The 700 Taels Mark. Then Major Players Came Forward to Enter Again, and The Foreign Exchange Rate Eased to Flat. However, The Turbulence Was Abnormal. When A Sudden Storm Arose, There Was News of A Conflict Between Japan and Russia, and Then The Selling Pressure Intensified. Moreover, The Indian Exchange Rate Was Large, Plunging Twenty Taels. The Afternoon Market Was Initially Stable, But Then Suddenly News Spread That Japan Was Going to Prohibit Gold Exports. The News Spread Through The Market, Causing Great Panic, With Clouds Covering The Sky, and A Feeling of Worsening Day By Day. It Plunged More Than Thirty Taels and Returned to The Lowest Price of The Morning, Only 672 Taels. The Selling Pressure from All Sides Increased Sharply. However, Because It Was Wednesday, There Was No Market for Drafts. In The End, It Seemed to Turn Slightly Flat, at 76 or 77 Taels. However, The Recent Market Price Fluctuations Have Been Huge and Large, So The Exchange Has Temporarily Added A Special Margin of Fifteen Taels, For A Total of Forty Taels.

Early Opening Immediately Drops, Then Chaos: The November Opening in The Morning Immediately Dropped 7.5 Taels, To 686 Taels (However, The Initial Gross Price Was 89 to Over 90 Taels, Which Was Done Towards Goods). The Long Term Continued to Rise One Penny, and American Silver Instead Fell Five-Eighths, So The Gold Price Did Not Plunge. If The Long Term Does Not Rise, It Will Definitely Open High, Then Increase to 90 Taels. However, All Parties Were Selling, Plunging More Than Ten Taels. At 9:00, It Was 71 Taels. Then Retailers Covered Their Shorts, and Shunli, Wanxing, Etc. Competed to Buy, Immediately Rising More Than Twenty Taels. The Foreign Exchange Market Was Incredibly Chaotic, Reaching 92 Taels at 9:20. It Was Later Learned That The Senior Commissioner Was Hanging Long, and It Retreated to 85 Taels. As Expected, The Price Was Hanging One Notch Higher, But American Gold Instead Shrank 0.25, and Japanese Gold Rose More Than 7.5 Cents, So The Gold Price Did Not Fall Further. Later, Buyers Were Also Active. Gan Changxiang, Hengxing, Chengfeng, Yongcuichang, Yongda Lianbang, and Goods Were Rushing In, Gradually Exceeding 700 Taels. However, A Few Taels Up and Down Was Nothing Strange. Until 11:00, It Reached 710 Taels. Guang Bang Yifeng Was Entering at A High Price. British Gold Fell from 15.8125 to 125. Retailers Were Selling Later. At 11:30, News Suddenly Came That A Dispute Had Broken Out Between Japan and Russia on The Middle East Route. People's Hearts Were Immediately Frightened. Tong Taichang, Hengxing Yuanmao Yong, and Speculators Like Mr. Wu Were Selling In Succession, Breaking 700 Taels In An Instant. Then It Was Heard That The Indian Exchange Rate Had Risen Sharply By One Rupee and Four Annas. At Noon, It Ended at 91 Taels. However, There Were 4 or 5 Taels Turning Over. The Noon Collection Was 98 Taels, and It Was Raised Again to 703-4 Taels. Then Goods Were Entering, But The Storm Was Terrible and Difficult to Grasp. The Opening Price Was Changed to 797 Taels and 4 Cents, With More Than 100 Taels Being Pressed.

Afternoon Initially Flat, Then Wild Fall Before Closing: The Afternoon Market Opened at 701 Taels, Followed By 08 Taels. The Market Situation Was Still Firm. Before Long, The Downward Trend Started Again. Because News Spread That The Japanese-Russian Situation Was Urgent, Major Players Were Selling Off One After Another, Such As Yuanmao Yong Dada Cheng Tong Taichang, Etc. Also, The Indian Exchange Rate Rises Again By One Rupee, So It Plunged Sharply. At 3:00, It Was 697 Taels. Hengxing Neixing, Etc. Were Buying, and In A Moment It Increased to 703 Taels. After 3:30, A Gloomy Cloud Covered The Sky, and The Air Was Extremely Bad. Suddenly, News Spread That Japan Had Lifted The Gold Ban and Closed The Outflow of Cash. People's Hearts Were Immediately Empty. Then Yuanmao Yong Zhifeng Yong Yifeng, Etc. Were Trying Their Best to Sell. Buyers on The Table Were Retreating and Avoiding It, Already Showing A Trend of Falling Down and Not Rising Again, Plunging A Huge 30 Taels. At 4:15, It Was Only 72 Taels. At This Time, Scattered Shorts Came to Catch Up and Enter, Immediately Rising 10 Taels, to 82 Taels. Then Lianbang Sold Off, and It Was Suppressed Again to 75 Taels. Tong Taichang, Etc. Entered Again, at 79 Taels. But People's Hearts Were Extremely Anxious, Suddenly Uneasy and Confused. At The 4:30 Closing, It Was 76 Taels and 5 Cents, Still Falling 17 Taels Compared to The Previous Day. It Has Fallen Continuously for Four Days, Reaching More Than 100 Taels. The Highest Price of The Day Was 710 Taels, The Lowest Price Was 671 Taels, A Difference of 39 Taels, But Slightly Flatter Than The Goods on The Previous Day. The Early Market Was 89 Taels, The Noon Collection Was 703 Taels, The Afternoon Was 03 Taels and 5, The Closing Was 77 Taels and 5. The Opening Price Was More Than 120 Taels Being Pressed. The Account Was Made Up, With The Front Market at 98 Taels, The Back Market at 77 Taels, and Red Strips Increasing By About 8.5 Taels.

The In and Out Are Complex and Difficult to Describe: The Tree Surface Transactions Are Confusing. According to Statistics, Shunli, Gan Changxiang, Yuankangxiang, Cuichangyong, Chengfeng, Yong, Etc. All Entered. Hengxing, Wanxing, Yuantai, Futaiheng, Dada Cheng, Yifeng, Yuanheng, Etc. Were Quite Busy Entering and Exiting. Zhifeng Yong Entered After Exiting First.
